Important Foreign Dispatches

British Labour Party Suffers a Crushing Defeat in the General Election 62

Occupying only fifty seats in Parliament

The contrast with the previous session is stark

Reuters, London, 29th - Of the former cabinet members of the previous Labour government who resigned from the cabinet when Prime Minister MacDonald formed the National Government, a total of sixteen, with the exception of the Minister of Works Lansbury and the Attorney General Cripps, have now been defeated. Therefore, important figures of the Labour Party will disappear from this new parliament. The cabinet members of the National Government, with the exception of the Minister of Finance Snowden and the Minister of Justice Wauchope, who had already stated that they would not stand for election, were all elected. Although MacDonald was expelled by the Labour Party branch in the Seaham constituency, he was still elected with 28,978 votes against 23,027 votes. It is noted that the House of Commons, including the university constituencies, has a total of 615 seats. At the time of dissolution, the number of seats for each party was as follows: Conservative Party 263, Labour Party 268, Liberal Party 58, National Labour Party 13, Independents 13. Of the 608 seats that have been declared, only seven constituencies are left undeclared. Of these 608 seats, the Labour Party occupies only 50 seats, which is a stark contrast to the previous parliament. Almost a complete wipeout, and these 50 seats are only for non-important figures in the Labour Party. The government party can be said to have won a complete victory this time. Even the British people who read the newspapers this morning were shocked by the crushing defeat of the Labour Party. None of the existing Conservative Party members were defeated, which is truly an unprecedented record for any major political party in Britain. Apart from the 50 seats of the Labour Party and the three seats of the Independents, the remaining 555 seats all belong to the National Government Party.

MacDonald Thanks the Nation for its Assistance 63

Prime Minister MacDonald has now issued a statement, informing the whole country, stating that the government has obtained an unprecedented majority, which will surely make the world know that the British people, when the nation asks for assistance, always respond with one heart and one mind. He further asked the people of the country to not only trust him, but also to be patient. As the people of the country know the difficulties of his work, he also wishes to give them full evidence that the government will work sincerely and strive together to find the best way to overcome the current difficulties. To the politicians who have suffered tremendous defeats and who have helped him to victory with their loyalty and courage, he wishes to say that their victory does not mean that he will ignore the interests of the working class when carrying out his current work.

Snowden Says It's Not a Party Victory 64

Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden also issued a statement to the people of the country, saying that Britain's position in the world will be greatly strengthened by this election. The result of this election is the greatest proof of democracy. The majority supporting the National Government is not that of one party, but a victory for the nation. This result gives the government the power to speak for the nation, but not to achieve its goals for one party.

Baldwin Expresses Satisfaction 65

Conservative Party leader Baldwin also issued a statement, saying that the country has won a great victory, but it is a pressing announcement by the British people as a whole to support national cooperation in order to restore the happiness of the country. The impact on foreign public opinion cannot be underestimated. The great support obtained by the National Government will resonate throughout the world and reaffirm its confidence in Britain's stability and greatness. Democracy has now expressed itself in a very remarkable form. The patriotism of our people has now been revealed to the outside world. When voting, the people of the country have declared in a clear voice that the doctrine of party strife cannot stand against the general desire for national cooperation in times of national emergency. The nation's workforce now trusts the National Government. He will certainly not let their trust down.

Conservative Rule is Conditional 66

National Liberal Party leader Samuel stated that great power in Parliament is now in the hands of the Conservative Party leader, but this is conditional, that is, this great power is given to the cabinet members of the National Government to handle the jointly agreed-upon undertaking, not the undertaking of any one party.

Labour Party's New Leader Groans in Bed 67

The defeated Labour Party leader Henderson issued a statement from his sickbed today, saying that the success of the party in power has far exceeded the most optimistic expectations of its leaders. The voters have been deceived by the "They want your money" slogan.

Japan Forces a Smile Through Tears 68

Reuters, Tokyo, 29th - Although Japan hates Britain for not supporting Japan in Geneva, Japanese newspapers and party leaders have unanimously praised the results of the British election, believing that this result can show the stability of the British people's thinking and their determination to restore their position in the world. It also said that the result of the British election represents a change from social idealism to patriotic pragmatism, and Japan should bear this lesson in mind.

Jiji Press, Tokyo, 29th - In the British general election, the Conservative Party won a great victory. As a result, the lifting of the gold export ban, which the whole world is watching, seems to be proceeding with the old parity method. The exchange rate of the pound will therefore be stabilized, but on the other hand, there is the threat of raising tariffs, and if the scope of preferential tariffs is expanded, Japanese traders will be greatly affected.

Russia Worries About Changes in Relations 69

Reuters, Riga, 29th - Moscow was shocked by the results of the British election. The Conservative Party's great victory has now caused anxiety about Anglo-Russian relations. A dispatch from Moscow said that officialdom refers to the British people's psychology as unpredictable and believes that previous claims of unrest in Britain cannot be relied upon.

German Public Opinion is a Mixture of Worry and Joy 70

National Press, Berlin, 29th - In the British election, the government party won a great victory. German public opinion has mixed feelings about this. What is pleasing is that since a stable government has been established in Britain, the country and abroad will benefit from it. What is worrying is that after the establishment of the Conservative government, it will inevitably adopt an active tariff policy. In today's free trade Britain, Britain is the main market for German products. If protective tariffs are implemented, German industry and commerce will inevitably be greatly affected. The above feelings are commonly expressed by ordinary German newspapers. However, the right-wing newspapers generally think from a political point of view, so they unanimously express joy at the victory of the British government party. For example, the Local Indicator newspaper even claimed that the British Labour Party was the source of all kinds of difficulties in Britain today and has been defeated by the public outrage of the people. Like chaff in the wind, it will be blown away in an instant. The newspaper also praised the British political system for being superior to others. Such a sound and noble election system is really second to none in the world. Other conservative newspapers also expressed unlimited joy at the British election and praised the soundness of the British people's political thinking. However, liberal newspapers, in addition to recognizing the correct actions of the British people in the British election, also suspected that this change was not enough to save the world's crisis and predicted that after several years of right-wing autocracy in Britain, the Labour Party would make a comeback. Furthermore, the protective tariff policy, which has become a fact, is even more likely to cause the Germans to be fearful. As for the socialist newspapers, they still try their best to encourage the Labour Party and do not recognize this election as an absolute failure.

French People Praise Extensively 71

National Press, Paris, 28th - Except for the newspapers of the Socialist Party and the Communist Party, the French newspapers still expressed great comfort at the victory of the Conservative Party in the British election. The Times said that this is a great sign of international order and national unity. MacDonald and Snowden did not hesitate to take the country as the most important thing in the national crisis, which can be said to be both intelligent and brave. The results of this election have further confirmed this. The Debate newspaper analyzed the results of the election, saying that many Liberal Party members who opposed the protective tax policy in the past and today also voted for the Conservative Party candidate for the sake of the country.

Labour and Management Jointly Petition the Government for Relief

Jiji Press, Tokyo, 29th - The Kobe Maritime Cooperative Association held a joint labour-management meeting yesterday to discuss the current situation. Japanese shipping has been affected by Britain's suspension of the gold standard and the Manchurian Incident. Ships will reach 1.5 million tons. Remedial measures such as operating funds and subsidies for ocean navigation have not helped the shipping industry. At present, the only remedial measure is for labour and management to jointly rescue more than 10,000 unemployed sailors. The association will recommend representatives to the government.

Japan's National Treasury Revenue Decreases Sharply 73

Difficulties in Compiling the New Budget

Jiji Press, Tokyo, 29th - The Japanese Ministry of Finance announced the national treasury accounts as of the end of June, with revenue of 110,243,000 yuan and expenditures of 177,388,000 yuan. The tax revenue was 48,800,000 yuan, a decrease of 8,306,000 yuan compared with the same period last year. The reason for this is the poor economic situation, which has led to a reduction in income tax, liquor tax, customs duty, and business income tax. Stamp tax revenue decreased by 1,028,000 yuan compared with the same period last year. Revenue from state-owned property and miscellaneous income also decreased across the board. In terms of current affairs alone, there was a decrease of 10,237,000 yuan in three months of this year.

Jiji Press, Tokyo, 29th - Finance Minister Inoue visited the Army Minister this morning to explain in detail the financial difficulties of the country. Regarding the compilation of next year's budget, considerable consideration must be given. He asked the Army Minister to try his best to reduce the budget by another 10 million yuan. Afterwards, the Army Minister immediately convened the heads of the Ministry of the Army to discuss this issue, hoping to meet the wishes of the Finance Minister, but it seems that it will not be possible in the end.

Rome City Opens All Night

Many places hold public works today, such as the completion ceremony of schools, bridges, and new railways, to commemorate the event. There is a largest new-style merchant ship in Trieste, weighing 48,000 tons, which will be launched today. The ship was built on the anniversary last year and will be completed next year. In the future, it can win glory for Italy on the Atlantic Ocean.

Zhang Haipeng's Attempt to Attack Longjiang (2) 79

Welcoming Representatives Have Been Released

But Attached with Compromise Conditions

Harbin Communication, After Zhang Haipeng learned that the provincial army had mobilized to resist, he retreated and adopted a defensive posture. The two sides confronted each other across the river (because the Jiang Bridge has been blown up). Zhang's rebellious army took Tailai County as the first line of defense. However, its main force did not move out at that time. Only 1,500 people who were repairing river projects were temporarily formed into an army and used as a cavalry vanguard force, deployed on the front line. This action was very embarrassing, because Yuan's brigade of the Tunken Army stationed in Tachengzi (now reorganized into a division) has already revolted, controlling the back of Zhang's army, and there was also a collapse within Zhang's army. If there were no Japanese troops as reinforcements, Zhang's army would have been like a turtle in a jar, and it would not have been difficult to capture it in one fell swoop. Now Zhang himself is still stationed in Taonan and ordered his eldest son, Zhiming, to be stationed in Tailai. Zhendong County is also under its occupation, so Zhang still occupies the land of three counties. On the afternoon of the 21st, there was another contact between the two sides. After a fierce battle for three hours, with the Japanese army assisting in the battle and firing artillery, Zhang's soldiers were unable to support and retreated. At 11:00 a.m. on the 22nd, four Japanese planes flew to Daxing Station (about 16 miles from Angangxi) and dropped eight bombs, seven of which exploded. Fortunately, one large bomb landed on the sand and did not explode, so only one or two soldiers were injured. Chairman Ma Zhanshan has taken over today (22). The ceremony was very simple. After the ceremony, he held a military meeting. The overall principle was to fight, and there was a saying that the Jiang Bridge should be repaired immediately in order to attack. Today, Vice Commander Zhang forwarded Zhang Haipeng's telegram, intending to clarify his intentions and that he had no intention of seizing Jiang Province. However, it was said that he was surrounded by the Japanese army and could not bear the coercion, which also showed his lack of reason and words. However, the matter is obvious and cannot be saved.

Yang Xiangqiu (Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce) and other eight representatives of various legal entities who were recommended to go to Taonan to welcome Zhang Haipeng the day before, because the provincial authorities temporarily received an urgent telegram from Vice Commander Zhang, insisting on fighting, had to change their position and actively resist. Zhang was very angry when he heard the news on the way, and he almost wanted to vent his anger on the representatives and poison them. Later, after all kinds of explanations, it was said that the mission of the representatives was only to represent the meaning of the local people. The only purpose was to hope to maintain peace and avoid starting a war. As for the proposition of the Beiping side to change the local officials by order (at that time, except for Chief of Staff Xie and Deputy Adjutant Tang, other important figures had temporarily taken refuge), it was really impossible for the representative power to prevent it, etc. Only then did Zhang understand a little, but he was still angry, so he did not release the representatives back to the province for a while. It was not until the 20th that a trusted friend named Jiang Mingjiu, who was also over 60 years old, was sent in a private capacity to accompany the representatives back to the province, taking the road of Changchun Harbin. It was heard that he secretly carried the mission of mediation and compromise. Among these eight representatives, Wang Jingxiu (Provincial Government Counselor and Director of Education) was left as a hostage. It is not known what it is for. On the 22nd, the new Chairman Ma specially convened a meeting for this matter and decided to recommend Ma Zidan (member of the Provincial Government) and others to accompany him to Taonan to exchange opinions. (24th)

News from the Harbin Press World: Reception for Foreign Journalists 80

Reporting on the Situation of the Northeast Under Japanese Occupation

Speeches from Newspaper Reporters

Harbin Dispatch: In order to allow foreign newspaper reporters to understand the true situation of the Japanese military's atrocities, reporters from newspapers in Harbin held a reception for foreign newspaper reporters from Harbin at the Huae Hotel in Daoli on the afternoon of the 23rd. More than 20 reporters from various newspapers attended. Li Pei of the Guowen News Agency was elected chairman, with Liu Tianyou of the Guanghua News Agency and Liu Quansun of the International Association News Agency serving as English and Russian translators, respectively. The foreign reporters attending included Ivanov and Genasinoff of the Russian-language newspapers, Ms. Irene, a special correspondent from the Chicago Daily News of the United States and the Shanghai Millard's Review, Masugowan of the Harbin Daily News, Bereske of the Harbin Xinbao, Gao Fuman, Kalikin, and Yenov of the Russian-language Ruble Newspaper, Kuolopakce of the Russian-language Donghua Newspaper, Furet of the English-language Daguan Newspaper and the British Asian Agency, Milik of the Russian-language Public Newspaper, and Niechijin, a resident reporter from the Soviet Daily Newspaper in Harbin. After the meeting was opened, the chairman delivered a speech, saying, "We are very honored that you gentlemen have deigned to come today. To be frank, there are many people in Harbin, but there are only a few hundred Chinese and foreign colleagues in the industry. We had long planned to fulfill our duty as hosts, but we have been constrained by various matters and have delayed until now. We are truly sorry. Unexpectedly, international justice has recently been trampled on, and world peace is in imminent danger. However, we are still very pleased to gather with you gentlemen. Regarding the Japanese military's invasion and occupation of Liaoning and Jilin, Moscow newspapers have unanimously called out, 'The real struggle is still to come.' You gentlemen have lived in Harbin for a long time and have more accurate knowledge. You must have a deeper understanding of the situation in China. Moreover, today is already the ninth day since the Japanese military violated the League of Nations resolution of the 30th of last month, which required them to withdraw their troops by the deadline. We have specially prepared refreshments to report on the truth, not only for your use in future historical records, but also to clarify right and wrong and maintain justice, just like your general mobilization. We would be especially grateful if you could offer your guidance." After the report was finished, pre-prepared report documents were distributed. Sun Shaoxian, a reporter from the Public Newspaper, read them aloud once. Subsequently, Furet, a reporter from the English-language Daguan Newspaper, delivered a speech, saying, "Although I am not Russian, there are many Russians here, so I will give my speech in Russian. In addition to deeply appreciating your hospitality, what I want to say to you gentlemen is that I have been engaged in the news business for many years and have connections with major newspaper offices in various places. I had long planned to get close to Chinese newspaper reporters, but I did not have a suitable opportunity. Today, I have this opportunity to meet with you all. Although what I want to say cannot represent all the guests, I believe that expressing my opinion in my individual capacity will gain the sympathy of most people. We record news and focus on facts. You gentlemen can understand by reading the records of the Harbin correspondence in the English-language newspaper. Two weeks ago, there was a similar opportunity in Beiping, where Chinese and foreign newspaper reporters could gather together. At that time, one reporter said that it was very difficult to get news from China, but the Japanese side fully supplied materials. Today, I am very grateful for your reports. Although most of the things reported have already been reported and published, I still intend to select and publish the reports in correspondence to various newspapers in England for publication. In the past, foreign news telegrams were not obtained from China, so naturally there was not much benefit for the Chinese side. Therefore, I hope to be close to Chinese reporters often, so that I can obtain truthful news from the Chinese side and understand the opinions of the Chinese people, so that I can report to various newspapers in England." The reporter from the Ruble Newspaper delivered a speech, saying, "If newspaper reporters have a powerful union, its power will naturally be great. I originally had a plan to connect Chinese and foreign newspaper reporters in Harbin and organize a union, but I did not have a suitable opportunity. Today, I have this opportunity, which may be the basis for the success of this matter. In the future, it may be put into practice. This kind of organization has great benefits. It can exchange news, obtain accurate news, and hope to achieve the goal of freedom of speech, as well as other mutual benefits. A Russian proverb says, 'Silence means acquiescence.' However, because we are restricted, we cannot have full records. We foreigners are here as guests. Since we have received the hospitality of the host, if the host is unwilling to express opinions, then it will be very difficult for newspaper reporters to visit various agencies to inquire about news. Therefore, it is easiest for there to be inappropriate things in the published news. Recently, the Party Department invited foreign newspaper reporters to express the attitude of the Chinese people, which is very clear. They can be called comrades in distress with Russia, so Russians express great sympathy for your countrymen." The reporter from the Donghua Newspaper delivered a speech, saying, "Although I am a Russian reporter, I work for the Russian-language edition of a newspaper in China. Since the Japanese invasion and occupation of various parts of the Eastern Provinces occurred, we have expressed our opposition to this action by Japan and supported the rights of China. Although the Japanese military has full equipment and great self-confidence, I firmly believe that in the future, justice will surely prevail, so the final victory will ultimately belong to China." The Soviet newspaper reporter gave a speech saying, "As for what the Chairman said about the Moscow newspapers, I am afraid that the Soviet newspapers are not easily available locally, and if you want to know the attitude of the Soviet newspapers towards China, you can read the newspapers issued by the Soviet Union elsewhere, and you will understand, and the attitude of the Soviet Union towards China, or Chinese and foreign journalists all know, can be said to be expressing full sympathy and goodwill towards China, and the Russian and Russian newspapers in Harbin may not be able to truly support the rights of China, and at the same time, the enemy of China is also publishing Russian newspapers in Harbin," the United States Chicago Public Newspaper reporter gave a speech saying, "I represent our newspaper and the magazines we serve and express our hope that Chinese and foreign journalists will exchange materials with each other, so that they can have an accurate record, and I have the utmost trust in your report, and I hope that you will work hard to get out of the national difficulties." The reporters all gave speeches one after another, and the gathering dispersed after enjoying themselves. The main points of the report issued by the Chinese press on that day were divided into six points: (1) Japan's so-called "Manchurian and Mongolian disputes," (2) Japan's prior planning and preparation, (3) The course and present situation of Japan's invasion and occupation of the Northeast, (4) Japan's violation of international faith and destruction of international laws and treaties, (5) The objects of the Japanese military's invasion and occupation of Manchuria and the exposure of the second step of their conspiracy, (6) The attitude currently held by the Chinese government and the people. The full text is omitted due to its length. (23rd)

Overseas Chinese in the United States Are Enthusiastic About Anti-Japanese Sentiment 81

San Francisco Dispatch: Various groups and schools of overseas Chinese in the United States, due to the fact that the Japanese imperialists have invaded our country, occupied the Eastern Provinces, destroyed various city buildings, and massacred countless people, are deliberately violating international law and despising justice. Therefore, on September 27, they held an anti-Japanese propaganda conference at the Great China Theater to arouse the sympathy of overseas Chinese for anti-Japanese patriotism and to hold a parade. At 12:00 noon on that day, they gathered in front of the Kuomintang General Branch, lined up, and set off, going from Stockton Street to Sacramento Street, turning to Grant Avenue, and then to Jackson Street to the meeting venue. The parade used a white cloth banner with the words "Anti-Japanese Patriotic Propaganda Conference" written on it as the lead. Representatives of various groups and overseas Chinese all held slogans opposing the unreasonable aggression of the Japanese imperialists against Chinese territory and opposing Japan's extermination of humanity and massacre of compatriots. During the parade, the streets were crowded with onlookers. After arriving at the meeting venue, the meeting was held. Deng Yahun presided over the meeting. Those who spoke in succession included Huang Yunsu, Consul General in San Francisco, Huang Jintian, representative of the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Huiwen, representative of the Veterinary Student Association of Stanford University, Liao Junzhe, representative of the Sanyi Guild Hall, Zhao Fuqiao, representative of the Yanghe Guild Hall, and Wu Rui, representative of the San Francisco Branch of the Overseas Transportation Department of the Lianyi. Finally, the chairman read five proposals from representatives of various groups to the public and submitted them for voting. The entire venue passed the proposals. Then, they shouted the slogans "Down with Japanese Imperialism" and "Long Live the Republic of China" and dispersed the meeting. The five proposals passed were as follows: (1) Send a telegram to Representative Shi Zhaoji urging the League of Nations to uphold justice and sanction Japan for its unreasonable invasion of China. (2) Send a telegram to thank US President Hoover and ask him to continue to uphold justice and maintain peace in East Asia. (3) Send a telegram to the National Government, requesting that Japan withdraw its troops within 24 hours and return all occupied areas, compensate for losses, otherwise, please use force to expel the Japanese invaders from the country, and absolutely refuse to directly negotiate with Japan. (4) Send a telegram to the Shanghai Press Association to forward to various people's organizations throughout the country, asking them to work hard to prepare for military affairs and use force to expel the Japanese invaders from the country. Our overseas Chinese swear to be the backing. (5) Please invite Mr. Hu Zhantang to take charge of the overall plan and jointly resist foreign aggression. (September 28)

The Increase in Coal Transportation Prices on the Jiaoji Railway 82

Qingdao Dispatch: The increase in coal transportation prices on the Jiaoji Railway has caused coal merchants along the line to rise up in opposition. The Shanghai National Coal Production and Sales Association also believes that it is not appropriate to increase prices during the promotion of national goods. Therefore, it recently sent a telegram to the Jiaoji Railway Bureau to inquire about the truth of the increase in coal transportation prices. The Bureau has telegraphed back to the Association regarding the circumstances of the case. The original telegram stated, "Regarding your telegram, the issue of coal transportation prices on this railway began in April of this year. We received an order from the Ministry stating that due to the soaring price of gold, expenditures on various railways have doubled. We were ordered to increase passenger and freight prices on various railways to make up for the losses. It was stipulated that passenger and freight prices on this railway would be increased by 20% across the board, and this was implemented on May 1. At that time, coal merchants raised objections to the coal transportation prices. Subsequently, Zhuang Shuting, representative of the Boshan Mining Industry Association, and Lu Da Company of the Qingdao Export Association, etc., sent a telegram on behalf of the company on April 4 and submitted a document on April 28. In addition, the Ministry of Railways sent a telegram on May 5, forwarding a document submitted by coal merchant representatives Cai Yiting, Ding Jingchen, Li Zumo, and Wang Shaoming, etc., all stating that the 20% increase in transportation prices should be complied with for domestic sales, but they requested exemption for exports. On May 30, Commissioner Ge of this railway was in Jinan. Coal merchants again selected Yang Yuan, manager of Lu Da Company, Ding Jingchen, manager of Yuesheng Company, and Zhuang Shuting, general manager of Tongxing Company, etc., as representatives to pay a visit, saying that coal merchants' business was light in the summer and requested that the export transportation prices be exempted from the increase during the summer. After the summer, an increase of 10% would be acceptable. Because there was a precedent for reducing coal transportation prices by 10% every summer on this railway, the proposed 20% increase was immediately used as a price reduction and submitted to the Ministry for approval. It was implemented on June 1. Subsequently, as the summer was coming to an end, the domestic sales transportation prices had already been approved by the merchants in previous documents and telegrams, so there was no problem. The export transportation prices were based on the coal merchants' statement that they could only increase by 10%. If they were required to increase by 20%, it would have an impact on foreign sales. Therefore, the export coal price was changed from 2 yuan and 5 jiao 2 fen to 2 yuan and 8 jiao, an increase of slightly more than 10%, which was in line with the amount stated by Yang, Ding, Zhuang, and others. After the proposed transportation prices for domestic and export coal after the summer were determined, they were submitted to the Ministry for approval and were ordered to be implemented after the end of the summer in late October. However, after the announcement, the coal merchants raised objections again. This is what this railway cannot understand. Your telegram stated that it is not appropriate to increase prices at the moment when national goods should be maintained. This case is a fact from May and did not happen now. We are honored to have been asked and have telegraphed back the circumstances for your reference." (October 27)

Suzhou 83

Provincial Agricultural Bank Business Conference: The fifth business conference of the Provincial Farmers Bank will be held today (30th) at the Bank Association in Hanjia Lane, Suzhou. Representatives from various branches must attend. The conference is scheduled for two days. Return of Confiscated Paper Goods: 158 pieces of paper goods that were successively confiscated by the Suzhou Railway Station were returned to the stores at 4:00 p.m. on the 29th by Wu Zhuxi, representative of the Chamber of Commerce, Chen Zulin of the County Party Department, and Chen Heqing of the Paper Industry Association. Three paper samples were extracted from each piece, and the respective business firms affixed their seals. Changshu 84

Discovery of a Large Gang of Bandit Ships Near Luyuan: At about 11:30 p.m. on the 28th, the armed agencies of this county received a telegram from Jiangyin, stating that a large gang of bandit ships had been discovered on the river surface near the Bayi Port, which is located at the junction of Yu and Cheng and close to Luyuan in this county. Among them were shallow-water gunboats and dozens of civilian ships, totaling nearly a thousand people, equipped with various firearms, such as machine guns. After receiving the news, this county immediately had Yang Qingjiu, captain of the 13th Water Police Team, telegraph the Yu Patrol Ship stationed in Hupu Port Town to be on alert. The garrison security team headquarters also had Battalion Commander Shen Yiming telegraph the Chen Company Commander stationed in Hu Village to lead his troops to the mouth of Xiansheng Bridge overnight to deploy defenses. At the same time, the county police team stationed at Quntangfang Bridge, after receiving the news, also concentrated at Xiansheng Bridge and cooperated with the security team to block the bandits.

Wuxi 85

The Situation of the Assaulting Police and Resisting Arrest Case Is Expanding: Xia Chunde, Director of the 16th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, sent nine people, including doctors Sun Deshun and Meng Qingfa, to the Zhu A Da teahouse in Yangting Town, 8th District, on the 12th of this month to arrest gamblers. Unexpectedly, Gao Yiqing and Deng Zuobi, the deputy township heads of the town, dared to instigate the gamblers to beat the police officers, causing injuries. Police officers Sun and Meng died due to their serious injuries. Subsequently, the County Court sent personnel to examine the bodies and confirmed the injuries. Coffins were prepared for burial, but the wives and brothers of the deceased, Meng Sun, and Meng Ying, believed that the district fee chief and the head of the branch office were largely responsible for this case. Therefore, they reported to the chairmen of the Yancheng Fellow Villagers Association, Jin Deyang and Liu Qidi, asking for assistance in seeking redress. Yesterday, Mr. Liu, together with the family members of the deceased, went to the Public Security Bureau to petition. Section Chief Hu came out to meet them on behalf of the bureau chief. Mr. Liu presented four points, asking for an immediate response: (1) The County Court has already confirmed that the deceased police officer Meng Qingfa died from injuries. Why did Branch Director Xia report that he died of typhoid fever? Was he injured or sick? (2) Taking a step back, even if it is acknowledged that Police Officer Meng was indeed ill, how could Branch Director Xia still order him to go out and arrest gamblers? (3) Such a large case of resisting arrest and assaulting the police is clearly a criminal offense. Why has the Public Security Bureau not transferred it to the court and only imposed a light punishment? (4) The most important thing in an assault case is to apprehend the murderers. The Public Security Bureau already knows the location of the murderers, so why has it not been able to apprehend them to this day? Section Chief Hu promised to forward the matter to Bureau Chief Hua to apprehend the murderers and seek redress.

Execution of Three Robbers: The County Public Security Bureau successively captured Gu Er'e, Xu Desheng (i.e., Xu Desheng), Hu Shijin, Zhang Xianda, and the ringleader Hua Yuquan (i.e., Ding Yuquan), five robbers who robbed Zhang Baoguan's home in Qingqiao Township, Jingyun City, and shot Zhang Liansheng. After presenting them to the County Government, County Magistrate Chen carefully studied the case. The robbers confessed to committing the robbery and sharing the loot. Based on the confessions, Chen believed that the three criminals Hua Yuquan, Gu Er'e, and Xu Desheng were more seriously involved and should be sentenced to death. Therefore, he telegraphed to the Department of Civil Affairs and forwarded it to the Provincial Government for review. After receiving the telegram, the Provincial Government believed that since the three criminals had confessed, they should be executed. County Magistrate Chen then ordered political police to bring the three criminals Hua Yuquan, Gu Er'e, and Xu Desheng from the detention center at 10:00 a.m. yesterday, verify their identities, bind them, and take them to the execution ground at the South School Field for execution as a warning.

Changzhou 86

Emergency Meeting of the Party Department After Wu Wenbi's Death: After Wu Wenbi, who was injured in the case of the destruction of the County Party Department in Wuyi, died at around 4:00 a.m. on the 28th, the County Party Department immediately convened an emergency meeting and decided on ten measures: (1) Report the details of Martyr Wu's death to the Provincial Party Department. (2) Send a letter to the county, setting a deadline and offering a reward to strictly apprehend the real murderers and bring them to justice to pay for their lives. (3) Telegraph the Provincial Party Department to consult the Provincial Government to order the county to strictly apprehend all the criminals, both principal and accessory, and bring them to justice. (4) Again telegraph the Provincial Party Department to consult the Provincial Government to quickly remove and punish Li Zonggang, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, who is sheltering reactionaries and neglecting his duties. (5) Schedule a memorial service for Martyr Wu to be attended by people from all walks of life. (6) Petition the Central Government for generous compensation. (7) Form a preparatory committee for Martyr Wu's funeral. (8) Convene the family members of Martyr Wu to discuss the aftermath. (9) Build a memorial tower for Martyr Wu's death. (10) Telegraph the Party Departments and anti-Japanese groups in various provinces and counties to report the details of Martyr Wu's death. It is also reported that Wu's body was examined and collected by the County Court and temporarily placed in the Qingliang Temple at 4:00 p.m. People from all walks of life welcomed the spirit coffin, and one person involved in the case, Jin Xiangsheng, was escorted back from Shanghai in the evening and is currently under investigation.

Zhenjiang 87

Verdict in the Case of Shooting and Killing an Innocent Citizen: The case of Zhu Jie, captain of the police team of the former Huaiyin County, shooting and killing an innocent citizen on September 26 of last year, was tried yesterday afternoon. Judge Yang, accompanied by Chief Clerk Wu, took his seat in the First Court and brought Zhu Jie, Li Yunpeng, and Liu Yunpeng to the court. After Judge Yang questioned the three defendants, he stood up and pronounced the verdict. Zhu Jie was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for each of the three counts of using violence and coercion to obtain confessions, deprivation of all public rights for two years, two years of imprisonment, and deprivation of all public rights for two years. The remaining charges were not guilty. The number of days in custody before the verdict was rendered was counted as two days for one day. Li Yunpeng and Liu Yunpeng were found not guilty. After the verdict was rendered, they were ordered to be returned to custody. Li and Liu could only be released after the appeal period had passed. It is said that Zhu had given up the right to appeal, but his intentions have not yet been determined.

Provincial Party Department Asks for Punishment of the Director of the Public Security Bureau of Wujin: The case of Wujin merchants gathering a crowd to riot, destroying the Party Department, newspaper office, and anti-Japanese association, and beating staff members Wu Wenbi and Lu Zao has already been decided by the Provincial Party Department to take five measures and has sent a letter to the Provincial Government for implementation. Now, according to a telegram from the Wujin County Party Department, Wu Wenbi died of his injuries at 4:00 a.m. yesterday. The Provincial Party Department deeply mourns Wu's sacrifice for the country. In addition to sending a telegram to Wu's family to express condolences and ordering the Wujin County Party Department to properly handle the aftermath, it also sent a telegram to the Provincial Government, strictly ordering the county magistrate to apprehend the murderers within a time limit and to remove and punish Li Zonggang, the Director of the Public Security Bureau of the county, to appease public anger.

Labor Dispute Occurs in the Weilun Factory: Since Yuan Yaomei withdrew as a shareholder, the Zhenjiang Weilun Silk Factory has received 22,000 yuan in maintenance funds from Shanghai under the name of Dingfengyong through the cocoon merchant Li Dongfu, preparing to start operations at a later date. Unexpectedly, a shareholder Zhang embezzled 18,000 yuan. Seeing that the funds were not available, Mr. Li dismissed the employees and entered into serious negotiations with Zhang. The general male and female workers, seeing Zhang embezzling the maintenance funds, went to Zhang's house to make a scene several times. Later, Mr. Li returned to Shanghai to recruit shareholders. After returning to Zhenjiang yesterday (28th) morning, the workers, believing that the recruitment was ineffective, went to Zhang's house again to question him and dragged Zhang to the Party and government agencies for negotiations. Later, a certain gentleman mediated the matter and promised to give a satisfactory reply today. Mr. Li also accused Zhang of embezzling huge sums of money, which led to the indefinite postponement of operations, and submitted a report to the various agencies for instructions, advocating for justice.

Reply from the Ministry of Education to the Petition of Students Returning from Japan 89

A total of five measures

It is reported that Mou Yu, a representative of the group of students returning from Japan, had a conversation with a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency. According to a certain staff member of the Ministry of Education, this record does not match the content of the conversation at that time. It is reported that three students returning from Japan, Cao Xiuxian, Mou Yu, and Tian Manyi (there was no Shi Wuwei), went to the Ministry of Education to petition, and a certain staff member of the Ministry of Education received them. The students presented various points, and they were answered separately. 1. Regarding the matter of sending all students studying in Japan back to China, the Chairman of the National Government issued an edict ordering the students to continue studying in Japan and not to return to China. The Ministry of Education has repeatedly ordered the Supervision Office for Students Studying in Japan to order the students to comply. (2) The Ministry of Education has a registration method for students who have returned to China. After registration, they will be sent to various universities to audit (not limited to national universities), and all expenses must be paid accordingly. (Students from free areas such as E, Xiang, Gan, Yu, Gan, Shaanxi, Wan, the north of Jiangsu, and the three eastern provinces can be handled according to the same regulations as domestic students.) (3) Whether provincial-funded students studying in Japan can transfer to other countries depends on the provincial governments. (4) The retention of student status in Japan for returning students must be determined after consultation with the Supervision Office for Students Studying in Japan. (5) The Ministry of Education previously ordered the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to provide some food and accommodation subsidies to students who have registered and have special economic difficulties, but not more than one yuan per person per day, until five days after the school is assigned. In addition, requests for returning home expenses and anti-Japanese work maintenance fees were all answered that there was no such method.

It is also reported that the Ministry of Education has been handling registration at the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau since the 19th of this month. As of the 26th, more than 50 students have gone to register. The Ministry of Education has ordered various public and private universities to allow them to audit temporarily according to their subjects and levels. The registration method is scheduled to end on the 28th.

Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of Various Universities 90

Six Important Cases Were Resolved

The Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of various universities in this city held its eighth representative assembly at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group at 2:00 PM yesterday, to discuss all ongoing matters. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below:

The meeting was attended by representatives from more than twenty universities. The representative from Jinan University served as chairman, and the representative from Guanghua University served as recorder. Formalities were observed, and reports were given by the chairman and various departments. The discussion then commenced. Representatives from the Municipal Party Committee were also present. Resolutions were made: (1) The entire group of executive officers were to select representatives to attend the National Student Anti-Japanese National Salvation Conference convened in the capital, and to decide on important principles. Resolved: (A) The representatives selected by this federation have the authority to attend the conference, preparatory meeting, and formal meetings. (B) The principles for proposals to the general assembly will be decided by the representative assembly, but representatives have full authority to make proposals within the framework of those principles. (C) This federation firmly advocates that the formal meeting of the Anti-Japanese General Assembly should be held outside the capital, with Shanghai being the most suitable location. (D) The units for the general assembly preparatory meeting should be based on the current geographical areas of student federations, while the formal meeting should be based on current administrative regions. The number of representatives from each unit should be proportional to the number of schools in that area. (E) Eleven school representatives were nominated to attend. (2) Regarding the establishment of a presidium and secretariat for the representative assembly, it was resolved that the representative assembly would not have a presidium but would establish a secretariat, with Fudan, Daxia, and the Law School jointly responsible. (3) Fifteen schools were nominated to form the presidium of the unified national assembly. Resolved: A vote would be held.

(4) Regarding the firm advocacy for requesting to attend the peace unification conference, it was resolved to pass the motion. (5) Regarding the dispatch of representatives with letters of explanation to inquire about the name, nature, and scope of the peace preparatory meeting, it was resolved to publicize the past experience of this federation in obtaining firearms, and to dispatch representatives (concurrently held by the representatives attending the Anti-Japanese Student General Assembly conference) to Nanjing to urge the release of firearms.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Commercial Library 95

Situation of Establishing a Book Lending and Delivery Department

The commercial library has collected a large number of books, which have always been open to the public. In response to the needs of readers, books have been available for loan outside the library for reading since the year before last. Recently, considering those who do not have time to visit the library to borrow books, a book lending and delivery department has been added. After various sectors learned about this, hundreds of requests for the regulations were sent to the library every day. The 5,000 copies of the printed regulations are about to be exhausted. This method is most sympathetic and gratifying to those who do not have time to leave their jobs and those who have lost their studies. A guarantee is attached to the regulations. Anyone who requests them can fill them out and send them back. As long as they pay a monthly transportation fee of two dimes or one yuan every six months, regardless of distance, and keep a catalog of the library's books, they can check out and borrow books without having to travel back and forth, without any effort. Any book they want to read can be delivered, which is very convenient. The establishment of this department by the library is truly convenient for many readers.

Professor Zhu Tongjiu of Jinan University Publishes New Book "Labor Economics" 96

Professor Zhu Tongjiu, a master of economics at National Jinan University, specializes in economics and has written books such as "Wage Theory," "Research Methods in Economics," and "Post-War Trends in Economics," which have long been circulated in academic circles. Currently, during his teaching breaks, Professor Zhu's new book, "Labor Economics," has been published by Liming Bookstore. The book is divided into twenty chapters, totaling more than 200,000 words. Its content emphasizes the economic background and changes in economic systems to explain the occurrence of labor movements. Secondly, it explains the changes in law, politics, and thought, and the labor movement, which are mutually causal. In other words, the changes in law, politics, and thought are affected by the labor movement, and the rise and fall of the labor movement are affected by law, politics, and thought. Thirdly, it describes in detail the internal organization of trade unions and the techniques of trade unions, and infers from local trade unions to national trade unions and world trade unions to clarify the trends of modern labor movements. Fourthly, it discusses the methods of resolving labor-management disputes, from which aspects to start, to provide government authorities with a reference for determining labor policies. Fifthly, it details the social trends in various countries and evaluates their merits and demerits. The entire book has a rigorous structure and fair arguments, and is considered a masterpiece in the field of economics in recent times. Therefore, Dr. Ma Yinchu commented that the book has the merit of clarifying the complex ideological trends in the country and has the effect of guiding young people's thinking on the right track. (Original text of Ma's preface)

This Year's Seventeen-Mile International Race Walking Scheduled 105

December 6th, Morning

The Shanghai International Race Walking Committee is actively promoting preparations for this year's competition, which is scheduled for the morning of December 6th. McKenna and Peasley, who was honeymooning in Pingdu, have both returned to Shanghai. McKenna has been promoting this sport for almost twenty years, and his enthusiasm has not diminished. Peasley is a well-known enthusiastic promoter. McKnodon, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, has agreed to serve as this year's president, and there are many other sponsors. As for the athletes, all parties are training very hard. At least twenty Chinese athletes are practicing diligently, and there are also five French athletes preparing to win. There is no shortage of people from England and Germany. The results of last year's seventeen-mile race walking are provided for reference by those who are practicing:

Free Talk

Voices of Anti-Japanese Sentiment

— Ju

"Clutching Buddha's feet in a crisis." This is the biggest problem of our people. Usually, they are muddleheaded and only know how to get by. Only when disaster strikes do they become anxious. Take this incident in the Eastern Provinces as an example. The Japanese had been plotting and scheming for more than just a year or two. I ask, what preparations did our country or its people make on a daily basis? Although our country claims to have 2 million soldiers, Chinese soldiers only have the courage to fight internally. When foreign aggression comes, they embrace a policy of non-resistance. Therefore, the people of various places, driven by righteous indignation, have risen up to organize volunteer armies. However, how can this kind of "clutching Buddha's feet in a crisis" organization withstand the organized and trained Japanese invaders? Therefore, I hope that in the future, on the one hand, the government should raise soldiers to fight externally and no longer engage in internal strife. On the other hand, the people should no longer engage in the "clutching Buddha's feet in a crisis" effort. There must be a permanent and definite organization. Only in this way can we resist foreign aggression and reject the Japanese invaders.

Essays by Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Industrial Civilization 108

In the autumn of the third year of the Republic of China, I took a sea voyage eastward for the first time. I said to myself: The sea vessel travels so fast, that's great. The textbook told me that this was powered by a steam engine, and I should go and see this steam engine. I went to the engine room to take a look for a while. I thought to myself, steam is water that has been boiled, so I have to go and see what is used to boil this water and how it is boiled. So I asked my way to the entrance of the firebox. When I took a look, several shirtless people were being roasted there like Tianjin ducks! Roasted with black oil all over their bodies! Their bodies, faces, and hands were as black as the coal they were burning! This was the impression I got from my first meeting with the stokers. It was like nitric acid engraved into my heart. I understood. The price of riding the long winds and breaking the ten thousand li of waves is the tears and blood of the stokers! And not just on the sea. The firebox is a hell on earth. If you go into a power plant, a machine factory, a flour mill, or a weaving factory, you will know that everything we eat, wear, and live in is permeated with the blood and tears of the workers! When eating a bowl of porridge, a bowl of noodles, wearing a piece of clothing, or lighting a lamp, we should think of how difficult it was to come by. If you don't have a chance to see it for yourself for a while, then please listen to me sing!

"The machine is running,

The furnace is red hot.

People and coal are very much alike!

Fat people go in and skinny people come out,

All going into the chimney.

Reducing a few hours,

Adding a few copper coins?

Workers are not happy in their work:

Adding this hell on earth,

To rebuild the heavenly palace."

The Past Records of Japan's Tribute and Invasion 109

— Qing Qu

The island barbarians in grass clothing were first seen in the Tribute of Yu. Since the Qin and Han dynasties, there have been few Japanese pirate troubles. This is because their customs love freshness and beauty, and their land is fertile and rich. The 573 counties all enjoy the surrounding sea. The rulers and ministers protect themselves and do not covet China. After Emperor Wu of the Han Dynasty destroyed Korea, they came to our country to pay tribute. (Korea belonged to Yan during the Warring States period. The Qin Dynasty established an outer border in Liaodong. When the Han Dynasty rose, it was difficult to defend due to the distance, so they repaired Liaodong. Therefore, the border reached the Pae River, which is east of Pyongyang, Korea, now called the Taedong River.) In the second year of Jianwu during the reign of Emperor Guangwu of the Han Dynasty, the King of Nu of Wa (Japan) sent envoys to pay tribute. In the first year of Yongfu during the reign of Emperor An of the Han Dynasty, he also sent envoys to pay tribute. In the third year of Jingfu during the reign of Emperor Ming of the Wei Dynasty, he sent the Daifu (official) Nan Shumi to pay tribute again. During the reign of Emperor Wu of the Jin Dynasty, he also entered to pay tribute. In the second year of Yongfu during the reign of Emperor Wu of the Song Dynasty, the King of Wa, Zan, came to court in person. In the second year of Yuanjia during the reign of Emperor Wen, Zan came to pay tribute again, and he established his younger brother, Zhen. At that time, he sent envoys to our country. In the twentieth year of Yuanjia, Zhen's son, Ji, succeeded and came to pay tribute. When Ji died, his son Xing succeeded and entered to pay court in the sixth year of Daming during the reign of Emperor Xiaowu. When Xing died, his younger brother Wu succeeded. In the second year of Shengping during the reign of Emperor Shun, he still sent envoys to pay tribute and presented memorials. After that, the rituals of paying tribute were continuously recorded in history. Those who saw the culture and artifacts of the Middle Kingdom and came to China to study, their ships were also constantly coming and going. There were even those who stayed for more than ten years before returning home. During the Sui and Tang dynasties, scholars and monks came to our country, with as many as five hundred or more people. Japan's admiration for the superior country can be said to be very prosperous. Since then, the culture of our China has gradually been transmitted to the three islands, and all laws and regulations have also been adopted by their scholars. Alas, how much did our China benefit the small island barbarians at that time? If they distort the past historical records and pretend to be friendly while carrying out acts of aggression, it is enough to stop them.

Japan's invasion of our sea borders began in the seventh month of autumn in the twenty-ninth year of Jiajing during the Ming Dynasty. They invaded eastern Zhejiang in the third month of spring in the thirty-fifth year. Zhao Wenhua and Hu Zongxian supervised military affairs to suppress the Japanese pirates. In the fifth month of summer, Zhao Wenhua was sent again to inspect the troops. In the eleventh month of winter in the forty-second year, the Japanese pirates captured Xinghua Prefecture. General Yu Dayou and Deputy General Qi Jiguang defeated them. In the fifth month of summer in the twenty-second year of Wanli, the Japanese pirates invaded Korea again. In the eleventh month of winter in the twenty-sixth year, the Japanese pirates began to flee. Our army pursued them in separate routes, and Korea was pacified. From Jiajing to Wanli in the fifty years, the Japanese repeatedly invaded us. At that time, Yan Song, a national traitor, held power and delayed military affairs to the point of decline, allowing the small pirates to be arrogant and domineering. However, he was still able to order generals and soldiers to eliminate the unrestrained ones and prevent them from invading again. He was also able to pacify Korea, to pacify the vassal states and appease foreign countries. It can also be seen that the sound and prestige of our China's punitive expeditions could still shake the universe. In the battle of the thirty-fifth year of Jiajing, more than 6,000 Japanese pirates fought for thousands of miles, lasting more than eighty days, and were finally annihilated by Cao Bangfu, the patrolling censor of Yingtian. Shen Liangcai succeeded him and reported the victory. Although later the jealous ones were greedy for merit and weakened their momentum, causing the Japanese pirate atmosphere to flourish again, the critics regretted it. However, our country put on armor and carried weapons in the vanguard, sacrificing their lives to kill the enemy on the battlefield, with more than 20,000 people. It can also glorify our national history and provide a spectacular sight for future historians. Alas, do those who now hold military power and control the military have any feelings about this? Although military matters are different now than in the past, and the relative strengths of China and foreign countries cannot be expressed through narrow-minded views, looking back at the past can also serve as a lesson.

### World News in Brief 110

— Hai Ke

A Factory Run Entirely by Women. In London, the capital of England, there is a factory that is entirely run by women, and men are not allowed to participate. This factory was jointly founded by twenty young women six years ago. They wanted to show the world some of their abilities and not think that this type of mechanical engineering business can only be done by men. The factory director is Ms. AAshberry, a member of the Engineering Society. There are only two female members in the society, and Ms. Ashberry is one of them. The craftsmen and even the clerks in the writing room are all women. Even the waiters who run errands and the salesmen who solicit business outside are all women. Since its opening, it has been extremely developed. Recently, it has signed contracts with the Aviation Department and the Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company to supply them with supplies. This is very rare. Ms. Ashberry once told reporters, "We are very proud to have such a factory in the country that is completely run by women. Our employees are not satisfied with just working in the factory. Several people have entered night school to study drawing, mathematics, and mechanics because they also want to become members of the Engineering Society in the future. Most of our work is to manufacture the most detailed accessories for airplanes and radios. We are indeed proficient in this way."

Remembering Mr. Tang Wei's Teaching Spirit 111

— Tang Keqin

At this time of national crisis, recalling Mr. Wei's earnest teachings, there is enough to revive the declining customs and save the mad tide. I will tell the world briefly. The teacher had gray hair and a bright spirit. He wore cloth clothes and ate simple meals. The distance between the residence and the lecture hall was about a mile. He walked to school. Even in the rain and snow, he never arrived late to school. How can he be compared with those who are still sleeping soundly when the sun is high? Before the bell rang, the teacher was already in his seat, lecturing and gesturing with all his strength. Whenever he read masculine texts, it was like a spring coming out of a high mountain, with wind and rain suddenly arriving. When reading feminine texts, it was like glory blowing in the wind, making people's hair stand on end. He encouraged people to set an example and said, "Scholars should be the first to worry about the world and the last to enjoy themselves." "Support yourself and do not ask for help from others." He encouraged people to go out and inquire about the world and said, "The people are my compatriots, and things are my companions." "Establish the heart for heaven and earth and establish a life for the people." He encouraged people to study and said, "Be diligent all day long." "Strive for self-improvement." He encouraged people to build their minds and said, "Sincerity never ceases." "The way of learning is to seek peace of mind." He encouraged people to save the country and said, "Sacrifice yourself for righteousness." "Give up life for righteousness." He especially emphasized integrity as the ultimate goal, so he selected the stories of Su Wu of the Han Dynasty and Zhang Xun of the Tang Dynasty who defended their integrity and died in hardship as a warning. How can they be compared with those who seek false fame in the world? The teacher said that the purpose of this school is different from the vulgar ones. Is this what he meant? I heard that the teacher is building school buildings and hiring learned people. If morality is lost and literature declines, there must be hope of revival. I am resting in Shanghai, witnessing the Japanese pirates' deceitful appearance. Remembering the teacher's merits cannot be erased. I will sharpen myself to learn from him.

Chronology of Japanese Aggression Against China and Various Massacres (6) 112

— Mo Yi

Republic of China, Year 17 (1928) (1) On the evening of February 18, the Japanese ship Atsuta No. 2 sank the Chinese ship Xin Daming at the Taixing port, drowning more than 100 passengers. The loss of goods exceeded 200,000 yuan. (2) On February 28, three Japanese warships fired guns in Dafu Port, killing and wounding more than 30 fishermen. (3) In April, Japan sent troops to Shandong for the third time to help the Feng-Lu army in the war. The Northern Expedition of the Revolutionary Army was greatly affected. On the 21st, the Japanese army used the excuse of protecting overseas Chinese to deploy defenses in Jinan. On May 1, they began to massacre Chinese soldiers and civilians. On the 3rd, a conflict with the Japanese army occurred due to the posting of slogans, which led to a massacre. Thousands of Chinese soldiers and civilians were killed. Cai Gongshi, a negotiator from our country, was also brutally killed. Countless radio stations and houses were burned down. (4) Japan rejected China's abolition of the Sino-Japanese Commercial Treaty that had reached its expiration date. (5) Japan obstructed the change of flags in the three eastern provinces, undermining China's unification. (6) A Japanese artillery vehicle in Hankou killed a rickshaw puller, Shui Xinglin.

Republic of China, Year 18 (1929) (1) The Tieling Incident. The Japanese army forced Lu Zhenwu, the director of the county public security bureau, to commit suicide. (2) Forced construction of the Jihui Road. (3) Japan opposed China's tariff autonomy.

Republic of China, Year 19 (1930) (1) In mid-April, Japan sent a large number of warships to China to conduct exercises in the Yangtze River basin, disregarding our country's sovereignty. (2) Japan excluded Chinese people from imports.

Republic of China, Year 20 (1931) (1) This summer, more than 200 Korean people suddenly came to Wanbaoshan near Changchun, Jilin. They rented land from Chinese people to engage in paddy field farming and dug the Yitong River to divert water to irrigate the fields, which greatly harmed the nearby farmland. The provincial government of our country ordered them to stop. The Koreans, under the command of the Japanese, ignored the orders. On July 2, Chinese farmers cut off their water diversion route because of their livelihood concerns. The Japanese incited the Koreans to massacre hundreds of Chinese merchants living in Korea in Pyongyang and other places on the 4th. Countless people were injured, and property losses amounted to millions of yuan. (2) September 18. (2) September 18. Japan used the disappearance of Nakamura and the destruction of the South Manchurian Railway by the Chinese army as excuses to send troops to Northeast China. Within a few days, they occupied the provinces of Liaoning and Jilin. Recently, they have used gunboat diplomacy to threaten China. This case has attracted international attention and is still under serious negotiation.

Yi An: This table is based on Bai Meichu's "Records of the Three Provinces of Manchuria," Wang Zhongqi's "Geography of This Country, Volume Two," Jiang Jianren's "History of Japanese Imperialism's Aggression Against China," the "Nanhua Review's Special Issue on Sino-Japanese Issues," and the daily reports of various newspapers. There are bound to be omissions. I hope readers will correct them. (End)

After Watching "Spring Scenery in the Singing Hall" 113

— Rui Hongchu

Amidst the sound of national crisis, we are not in the mood for entertainment. However, domestic films seem to be indispensable to promote. Recently, Tianyi Company created a domestic Movietone film, which was recently completed and released to the public at the New Grand Theater. I was invited by Mr. Tan Zhujun, the secretary of the company, to visit and watch. After watching it, I took up my pen and recorded it as follows.

The script of "Spring Scenery in the Singing Hall" was written by the famous novelist Yao Suifeng. Li Jinhui was also invited to specially compose the songs, which added to the splendor. Ms. Xuan Jinglin played the singer Li Huifang, gracefully appearing on stage and singing new songs of youthful joy. Her pearly voice was melodious and extraordinary, earning the audience's praise. Ms. Pu Jinghong played Huifang's maid Fanggu, and her singing was also clear and pleasant. Ms. Pu was burned by alcohol during filming and eventually died. Now the sound and image still exist, but the person is gone, making people sigh endlessly.

This year, our country's floods were extremely heavy, and many places became marshlands. The cries of the displaced were everywhere, which was unbearable to see. Therefore, the film interspersed with the Maritime Charity Groups holding a disaster relief performance. Mr. Zhu Ziqiao and Mr. Wang Xiaolai were specially invited to give speeches on the flood situation. Mr. Wang spoke in Shaoxing dialect, which made people laugh. Movie actresses were also hired. Ms. Xuan Jinglin sang "Jiangnan Hao" and "Picking Flowers." Ms. Yang Naimei sang "Cold Night Song." Ms. Xu Qinfang sang "Fragrant Grass Beauty Song." Ms. Wu Suxin sang "Su San Starts Her Journey." Ms. Zi Luolan performed the Zi Luolan Dance, and there were more than 20 male and female stars such as Chen Yumei, Lu Jianfen, Zhang Yongcui, Tao Yayun, Jiang Naifang, Qin Haha, Xiao Zhengzhong, Zhang Zhenduo, Chen Yitang, and Sun Min, which was quite lively. The clarity of the sound and the twists and turns of the plot were especially rare.

Rotary Club

A Countryman Goes to Shanghai Again (1) 114

— Tian Xiao

Ever since the countryman stumbled upon Shanghai last time, he had been thinking about it all the time. He mentioned Shanghai while eating, he mentioned Shanghai while sleeping, and he mentioned Shanghai while defecating. "No wonder those yellow-haired girls are reluctant to return to the countryside once they get to Shanghai. Even I, an old man, have been thinking about it all the time after visiting Shanghai. I really don't want to be so old and have fallen in love. It's not any other kind of lovesickness, it's just the lovesickness of missing Shanghai." In his spare time, he held a foot-long dry tobacco pipe in his hand, a purple clay teapot, barefoot, and with his chest open, sitting on a bamboo couch in front of the door, and proudly said to the neighbors who were enjoying the cool breeze and had never been to Shanghai. "Old uncle! When are you going to Shanghai again?" Two seventeen- or eighteen-year-old village girls, named Ashui and Jin, raised their heads, and their sun-yellowed hair was reflected in the sunset shadow, looking at him enviously. "Me? I'll be going soon. Ashui and Jin! If you go to Shanghai, you'll never want to come back again. It's a pity that your father and mother won't let you go," the countryman said with a hint of seduction in his tone. "We don't want to go to Shanghai," Ashui's mother said firmly.

"Why not?" the countryman asked.

"Shanghai is not a good place. The year before last, the young daughter (Note 2) of our Lord's (Note 1) family went to Shanghai to be a maid because her aunt was helping people (Note 3) in Shanghai. Who knew that later, she went to a performance house and refused to come back. That young daughter had already been given to someone else, and the man's family wanted to marry her, but later she even had a lawsuit. Our Ashui has been promised to Xiao Mao, the son of Ada in the front village, since she was three years old. Shanghai is not a good place, we don't want to go."

"There are also people who make a fortune. Didn't that Xiao Ayi send money to her brother last year to build a house in the countryside?" This was an old man named Xiao Di, sitting near the awning, drinking shochu and enjoying himself.

"Hmph! Where did Xiao Ayi's money come from? Wasn't it earned by being a prostitute and selling her body? Shanghai is a filthy world, and even the cars are strange. What's called a turtle car, a tortoise tram?"

"Ashui's mother! You misheard. It's not a turtle car, it's a rickshaw. It's not a tortoise tram, it's a trolleybus," the countryman laughed loudly, indicating that he was an old Shanghai resident and had seen a lot.

(Note 1) The villagers call Sun Age Lord (Note 2) Young daughter means young girl (Note 3) Helping people means working as a servant

Commercial News

Financial Standard Gold Continues to Decline Slightly 115

No significant changes. Yesterday, the 29th, the price of standard gold tended to decline, but there were no special changes. It consistently fluctuated by only six liang, and ultimately fell slightly by two liang. Dealers' attitudes remained uncertain, so demand and supply differed significantly. As for the silver market, it rebounded, and there were rumors that the United States was planning to convene a silver conference. Therefore, it opened at a low price. Afterwards, buyers seemed to be more active, probably because the foreign exchange market stabilized slightly and banks made some purchases, so it turned upward. It rose from 703 liang to 708 liang. However, Japanese banks seemed to want to sell British gold, and because of the relentless selling in the market, a state of demand weakness was revealed. The market was still relatively stable, but trading was light and quite mediocre.

Opened down by more than two liang. It opened in the morning and fell by 2.9 qian, to 705 liang. The big bar rose by one-eighth. The official and private telegraph prices of silver each rose by one-quarter. Then it fell from 5.8 qian to 0.25 qian because Zhifeng, Yongfu, Changyuansheng, Dadecheng and others were selling. Later, HSBC bought 30,000 US dollars of forward US dollars at 125 yuan and 32.0625 yuan of recent US dollars. Moreover, because Daxing, Yongyuanmao, Yonggan, Changxiang, Zhifengyong, and others were buying, and because banks were mutually doing this month's British gold at 5.625, it immediately increased by more than three liang, to 0.57 qian. The announced price of British gold did not move, at 0.5 liang. Then it added three qian. Because scattered households came out, it fell by two liang, to 0.37 qian. After 9:30, Yuanxingyong, Daxingyong, Hengchangyong, Hengyu, Tong Taichang, and others all bought in, and the market sentiment suddenly strengthened and rose upward. By 10:00, it had risen to 0.85 liang, but the exchange rate was flat. Chinese banks sold recent US dollars at 32 yuan, and arbitrageurs came to sell, so the price gradually decreased. Forward British gold could be settled at 1.75. Until after 11:00, it dropped to 0.48 liang. In this small hour, there were advances and retreats of one or two liang. After entering, HSBC absorbed this month's British gold at 5.615, Shanghai and others absorbed forward at 1.75, and there were some scattered short sellers, which led to a pull-up of two liang. At 11:30, it was 6.8 qian. Because Hengyu, Xiexingyong, and others sold, and said that British gold seemed loose, with recent gold settling at 5.625 and forward gold at half a penny, people's hearts turned downward, and it fell by four liang, to 0.28 qian at noon. Tong Taichang slightly advanced. By the time the market closed at 3.7 qian, it was again pushed up to 0.5 liang. Goods and others bought in. Afterwards, it retreated to 0.4 liang again. The announced price was still 767.8 liang, with a discount of about 60 liang.

The afternoon market was desolate. The afternoon market opened at 0.45 liang. Afterwards, it was bought by Yuanmaoyong and others, rising by more than two liang, to 0.7 liang. Then it was suppressed by a little more than one liang. After 2:30, it was 0.53 qian. The foreign exchange market was stable. Banks made two-month British gold at half a penny, and November US dollars at 32 yuan, which was higher than at noon. Afterwards, British and Japanese banks made transactions with each other, with forward British gold at 4.375, so the price of gold rose by two points. At 3:15, it was 0.65 liang. But the trading on the table was extremely quiet, so the industry had already made a game and urged to hang up the closing sign. Therefore, by 3:30, it was counted as 0.58 qian. The closing price was 2.1 qian lower compared to the day before yesterday. But the crowd did not disperse and still extended until after 4:30. Suddenly, there were transactions between the Dalian gangs, and the price was raised to outside 0.6 liang. Jinheng sold more than 100 bars to Tong Taichang, with the price at 0.65 liang. Unexpectedly, that company suddenly claimed that it had exceeded the exchange's regulations and would not do business after 4:30. It was decided to abandon the discussion. However, Tong Taichang had advanced for customers, and the phone had already been dialed, so the field account should be stamped. Therefore, they went to the council to request a judgment and argued for a long time, which has not yet been resolved. The maximum price of the whole day was 0.85 liang, and the minimum price was 0.25 liang, with a difference of six liang. The early market for goods was six liang, the noon closing was 0.45 liang, and the afternoon closing was 0.5 liang and a half. The announced price was reduced by more than 60 liang. The registered price was 0.4 liang, the water supplement was 0.4 liang in the afternoon, and 0.6 liang, and the red bar was added by 8.5 liang.

A glimpse of the industry's transactions. According to the statistics of the transactions on the table, Yuanmaoyong, Tong Taichang, Fuyu, Hengyu, Yuankangxiang, Hengchangyong, Shunli, Yuanxingyong, Daxingyong, and Yu Da all entered. Zhifengyong, Qianchangxiang, Xiexingyong, Yuantai, and Yifengyong had quite a few withdrawals. Fuchang, Yuansheng, Futaiheng, and Cuichangyong all withdrew. Dadecheng had a total of more than 2,000 bars and advanced more than 100 bars. In the afternoon, Yuanmaoyong and Tong Taichang slightly advanced, while Wanxing, Fuchang, and Hengchangyong withdrew. It was heard that foreign merchants Qiao Zhifu slightly advanced. The Dalian gang advanced a total of 1,000 and withdrew 400 or 500, still occupying the short side. The Guangdong gang did not move, it is said.

The Trends of Foreign Exchange Near and Far Differ 116

Yesterday, the British, American, Indian, and silver markets all rebounded, and the exchange rate also rose. The HSBC hanging price only reduced the exchange rates of France and Germany by one yuan each. Hong Kong added 125 to 77.75 liang. The others, such as British and American, did not change.
